After that, make two cauterizations on each leg, at the tip of the cutting knife; and perform the cauterization longwise, one on the inside of the knee joint and the other outside, along the leg; leave the cauterizations to heal for a long time without cleaning, until the wound has healed; then attend to the other treatments that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the fracture
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When the solution of the belly comes from cold and moisture, weakening the retentive and digestive virtues in the stomach and intestines, it cannot be cured by any treatment; and you see the patient enduring great suffering with powerful virtue, so apply a strong cautery on the stomach according to what has been said before about the stomach cautery, using careful and subtle cauteries around the anus, and two cauteries on the haunches.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see an abundance of moisture and the patient suffering greatly, apply a cautery to the wrist, and one cautery on each side, and several small cauteries on the stomach to remove the great pain, for the cure is beneficial when there is good help.
de la cure des emorroydes	On the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When hemorrhoids are of long standing and consist of corrupt, cold, and moist humors, they are treated as we have said in the previous sections, but the treatment is not effective if cautery is performed: Make three incisions along the spine of the back, starting from below the shoulder blade, making them slightly triangular, and one incision at the base of the anus (two incisions total); If you think that the patient's stomach is cold, the meat is not cooked, and swelling is visible on the face, then make a large cautery on the stomach as mentioned above, and another on the liver, and yet another across the entire area with cautery pins; Leave the cautery open for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment, reset the joint as long as it is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the fleshiness called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you deal with the fleshiness (thelul), if you feel the cautery seems too severe, then take a hot tool and apply it thoroughly to that flesh; leave it in place until the cautery is complete, from which the skin will heal; do this once or twice, and if there is much flesh, cauterize each part as we have said; afterward, treat the wounds profitably as long as they are healthy; and if you cauterize with a great cautery on raw flesh, it will bring greater aid.
de plaie mal curee	from the poorly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure cutting or opening, as we shall relate in its place, a certain illness comes about that can only be healed by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When a vein becomes fistulated, inflamed, filled with pus and corrupted moisture, you must try every subtle treatment, and be sure to understand the entire effect of each one as it unfolds.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After the cautery appears to be sharp enough, insert it into the fistula according to the amount of the attempt that entered, and repeat the cautery once or twice or three times, depending on the quantity required; and be careful not to burn the nerves and large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	He should probe with the fistula through the bladder and intestines, taking care of these openings, and only make fires over the fleshy parts, and think that it is not harmful; afterward, cure the opening as long as it remains healthy, and if the openings are closed and the matter has been drawn out for a long time, then know that the opening is entirely healed; and if the matter has not been drawn out, know that the opening is weak, and the bone is corrupted to the bottom; and thus, as we shall say of this in its place.
de la maladie des reins	On the disease of the kidneys.
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When the pain of a wound comes with heavy bleeding and great flatulence, and cannot be treated by women, then you must cauterize it on both sides with a hot clavicle, as we have previously mentioned; and if we cauterize it in the middle, there will be three cauterizations in line, and it will bring greater help.
de la vessie	Of the bladder" in Old French translates to "de
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is soft and weak from pain and moisture, so that the patient retains urine, then you should cauterize it on the outer part above the bladder, where the hairs begin to grow, both on the right and left side, making each cautery as long as a thumb; and also cauterize behind the back if necessary; and make the clavicle cauteries according to the shape previously mentioned.
de la marris	Of the joint
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the wound is cold and moist, it does not allow healing, and the flowers (scabs) are corrupted and their healing is slow; when they do heal, great pain is felt. Then it is necessary to perform three cauterizations around the wound, as we have said in the cauterization of the bladder, and two cauterizations on the back; and the cauterization should be done with a clavicle, as we have said.
de la hainche	de la hainche" translates directly to "of the spine
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When viscous moisture descends into the channel of the spine, and for this reason it moves out of its place, and the signs are that one leg is longer than the other when measured together; then it is necessary to cauterize the patient above the channel of the spine with a cauterization resembling a circle, and mark in front of the joint around the channel as it rotates, so that the channel remains within the circle; and the cauterization should be like that which was done on the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if this cautery is not present for you, perform three cauterizations with hot oil, and let the cauterization be just as effective as all the others; and treat the wound until it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When the pain comes in the back, and it is due to cold and moisture, and the patient is cured as we have said in the previous section, but the treatment is ineffective, and the illness is chronic: then you must purge the patient of the bad humors through foul pills, or other good-looking pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	Afterward, he applies cautery; and the manner of cautery is according to two methods: that is to say, collectively burning medicines, and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Fire cautery is performed according to many methods, of which some are: You cauterize along the ribcage in three places, making deep and broad incisions, with a space the thickness of two fingers between each cautery, and they are olive-shaped. One should never perform cautery in the middle of the chest, for there are three according to this form.
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you see that cautery should be performed in a circular shape as we have previously mentioned regarding the dislocation of the ribcage; but do it in such a way that the circles encompasses the entire ribcage, and all the spaces around the heart are burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the method used for sciatica, when pain persists in the hip and does not reach the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if the pain reaches the thigh and leg, apply a cautery to the affected area where the patient feels the most pain, either with a cut or by burning the thickest part of the tissue; and if the patient feels that the pain radiates up to two fingers' length from the sole of the foot or near it, cauterize there, three or four points, depending on the severity of the pain, and this cautery is called 'point'.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if it happens that the pain is so severe in the knee towards the thigh, then he should do cautery with a sharp or circular instrument, and be very careful in all his cauterizations that he does not leave them until he burns the nerves and large arteries, and do not cause the patient greater harm and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who have done cautery on the ankle of the foot, and left them until the leg was completely swollen, and the foot as well, and it became pierced and corrupted all over the foot.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After an abdominal solution, he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts together, perform cautery on one and the other according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the wise say about cautery for the hinch, which is how it should be done: take a piece of iron as thick as a new coin or slightly thinner, and make it twisted and interwoven from one side to the other with a space between them equal to the size of a thumb; intertwine them across each other, and they should be as strong, and have a well-made iron point; this is its shape.
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And heat it until it is completely red and smells foul, then place it on the wound of the sick hinch, and turn to the healthy side; cauterize once again after the first cauterization and leave for three days; then apply a poultice of butter, and keep the wound open for a long time; treat with care until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Albucasim says that we should use this cautery little due to the danger of its regard, and we see few who use it; nevertheless, these are good cauteries that the patient can endure, and where it is most suitable.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The burning cautery tools are such that you make an instrument with a descending edge along the margin of the door, either of iron or steel on a long pole. At the top, it should have a handle, and between each other, the thickness of two fingers; they should be open at both ends and joined together in this manner.
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After placing the board of the couch over the patient lying on their side, and quickly covering your hand with the board, pour between the two circles of hot ash that has been heated over fire for a little while, and leave it for an hour, allowing the patient to endure the heat and burns.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it has a true burning sensation like fire; and when the burns have subsided, gently lift your hand with the instrument and raise the affected limb with soft pressure, leaving it for three days, then apply butter until the blackening from the burn disappears; this would be the final aid after treating the wounds as long as they are healthy.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And if the pain extends to the thigh or leg, apply the instrument with pressure according to what you did with the limb, increasing it as needed; this is the method of hot compression, which I have written about in the treatment of fractures.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and quicklime, as much of one as the other, grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	If there is a small opening not blocked, let the tip of a razor enter; then place this pot into another well-sealed pot, and add alkali and lime, stirring gently until there are two layers of powder at the top, as you hold it firmly in your hand; leave it thus until all the water and impurities have settled to the bottom. Then take all that water, pour it over the lime and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	And thus it is very beneficial and proven in many medical works and cautery treatments for other parts of the body, as it acts like fire, and with other medicines such as foments, honey, anacardium, and lime with soap, all these mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a treatment that healed a noble of the pain in his back and sciatic nerve, and he says that no other cure was done, and it healed completely once this treatment was applied, and he bathed as he teaches below.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And he says to prepare a mixture of fresh and dry verdigris, grind it finely with some fat, apply it to the back and thigh and leg where the pain is, and wrap it; leave it for three hours or according to the amount so that the patient no longer feels the burning.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then make him enter or take a bath as long as the body is slightly heated, and make him lie down, and the pain will leave entirely and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use fire cautery with such medications unless it is after the evacuation of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Dyascorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat's milk, it provides great aid; and the cautery should be done in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take linen and grease it with old oil, and apply to the pit that is between the thumb and the toe of the foot, and also to the one called the fascicle.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	After taking a piece of dry sheepgut, ignite it in fire until it becomes ashes, and place it on the wound, leaving it until the wound is healed; and repeat this process, ceasing only when you think by sense that the pain has ceased; and this method of cauterization is called "sheepgut cautery.
de la dolor dou dos	of the intense pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from strain or impact, or excessive evacuation, or from a similar feeling of cold, expanded matter, none of these signs warrant cauterization, except for that which comes from the infusion of cold material.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary after that the patient be cleared of foul pills or other similar things, and that one make them on the back, where the pain resides, three lines marked with a signet, and in each line V cauterizations or more according to the virtue and quantity that the patient can endure; and the cauterizations are made according to the cautery called "point"; and if you see fit, do III cauterizations or IV at the middle cautery according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	This illness often strikes small children, and the signs of its onset are that they have a tight airway when breathing, and weakness; and you will find in the lower back a sharp pain that extends to the other parts of the back.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this, and you observe it being cured, cauterize it with the cautery iron according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	The cautery should penetrate each part of the wound equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see that the cautery penetrates around the wound with the iron, either two lines or three, and the points are close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After treatment, reset the limb as healthy according to what we have said, and be careful not to apply cautery to any numb areas that are affected by nerve damage.
de la dolor des jointes	Of the pain of joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When the pain of joints is caused by moisture that spreads throughout each member with great intensity, and when the pain comes on suddenly, they rightly call it "podagra", and when it is due to a cold cause and medicinal cures cannot heal it, then cautery is the cure in this manner: make several cauterizations around the joint of the foot, and let the cauterization be olive-colored according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if it is necessary to prick on the sole of the foot, let the cauterization be made with a point.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pains come up to the knees and other joints, this often occurs, so he should cauterize each knee with three or four cauterizations from each part, using olive oil cautery; and if you need more, you can do it, but don't hold your hand too tightly until the expected heat is achieved.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knees and back, apply the cauterization that we have mentioned in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains are in the hands, make two incisions around the fingers; and if no pain remains in the thumb, make incisions on each joint and even on the hair of the hand; and if the pains come up to the wrists or shoulders, cauterize each part, and apply proper care to the patient and take medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	Because if you provide proper care and drain the excess fluid, it will be healed by God's grace.
de la routure dou syfac	Of the dislocation of the shoulder
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When the dislocation occurs suddenly and the joints descend to their proper place, it is important that when you attempt to cure it, you do not manipulate it immediately; instead, use things that aid digestion so that the bowel movements descend. After that, have him lie on his back in your hands, and instruct him to hold his breath while you reset the joint, aligning them correctly and gently, and then re-locating the dislocated bone into its original position. Make a sign by drawing an image resembling half of a circle above the broken bone; then apply the hot cautery as described earlier.
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	as long as it is white and it sheds scales.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then reset the bones to their proper places; and have the attendants place their hands on him so that he does not move back; and open the thighs well for the patient, and place a cushion and a bolster under his thighs, and another one on his penis which holds his hands; then apply the cautery to the sign over your entire hand, and hold it straight and tight until you reach the bone, and if you do not touch the bone the first time, repeat it again until you do; and be careful that the bone does not move when you perform the cautery; do not burn him; and ensure that the patient does not die, or suffer any other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know this: if you do not go close to the bone with cautery, your work is useless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is necessary that the cauterization of children be subtle according to their size, and of adults as large as them; after three days, treat the wound with butter until the scorch is healed; after that, cure other wounds until they are clean, and lay the patient on his back for forty days until the wound is well sealed; and it is necessary that his movements be limited for a long time, so that the boils do not appear when he gets up to go to his room.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And after forty days, when he wishes to rise, a well-made bandage is applied to him and left for another forty days; and he should have good rest, working little and guarding against excessive drinking and eating, and from too much noise; and with this instruction, he will be completely healed.

de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the abdomen
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures occur in other abdomen regions and are recognized, and you see that they do not continue to grow, hold the cautery near the affected area according to its quantity, burning it with a third of the heart's beat; after the treatment, as we have said; and no among the ancients have stated that one should cauterize at three angles in this form:

de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of great pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain arises in any limb, whether from a fall or an injury, and this pain persists for a long time, and the medicinal cure is ineffective, then it should be cauterized with the cautery known as 'point', and the cauterization should be done according to the length of the member and its smallness and weakness, and its tendency to twist, and considering its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If he is healthy after the first cautery, that is well; if not, begin another cautery on that part, for often it is the adjacent limb that needs to move, so you must perform cauteries until the patient is healed.
de meselerie	It seems like there might have been a slight error in your

Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	You can treat it by cauterizing, taking care if the illness is in its beginning, and if it is cured according to what we have said in the previous division, without delay or hesitation, and you doubt that the corruption has spread throughout the patient, then make V cauterizations on the head: I on the top of the head, and the second at the end of the hair; and two on each horn, and one behind on the nape; and leave your hand so that the cauterization goes down to the bone, and as far as the skin comes out so that the vapors of the thick humors can escape; and cauterize it on the tongue according to what is necessary.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	And if the illness is widespread and manifestly severe, then it is necessary to apply these cauteries that we have mentioned above: first cauterize in the armpits, second on the spine of the neck, third on the spine of the back, fourth over the thigh and another gentle one on the shoulder blades; also two on the ribs, two on the tendons of the pisiform bone, and one each on the joints of the hands and feet, and in the fossae of the hands; be wary of the nails that are on the last toe, so as not to burn them. Never make a cautery on the bones of the wrist, or on the stomach bone, or on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And know that the more cautery is done, the greater the aid and benefit it brings, and drives away the illness; and know that the patient does not feel any pain from the cautery as the healthy do, because the body is already corrupt.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cautery be great or small according to the member and joints, as you will find in the ways of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treatment, apply a poultice of flour, honey, and other remedies until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When swelling appears in any member and is not cured by medicine, oils, poultices, or bandages, and it remains inflamed, then perform cauterization on the member according to its size and severity; and make the cautery slightly within the depth of the flesh; then apply treatments with oil until it is healed.

When the disease called "albaras" is ignited, and the medical arts are of no avail, then cauterize with a hot iron to the degree necessary until the blanching is removed and the color changes; afterwards, apply a cure made from flour, peas, lentils, with rose oil, plantain leaves, collicon (a herb), and alder bark, each part separately; mix all together, wrap it in cloth, and keep it on the affected area until it heals.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of a ulcer by cautery.
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When an ulcer appears at the beginning and you wish to stop it, cauterize it with a hot iron in a circular motion around the entire edge of the ulcer.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres. de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	from the flesh that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When anyone has a disease called "adubelati" and they do not want to die, or because of the excessive discharge it produces, or because of the old age of the patient and his frail condition (that is, too much), and he has little blood, or because of the time; and you see him hastening to die: then cauterize him around with many small cauterizations by pricking; after which leave him alone.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For she will hasten to die.

li cure dou feu par fer	Heal with fire using iron.
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	There is another kind of disease called "corrodens," which is nothing but a consumption of the limbs, for it wastes the members as fire does dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in a limb that can be treated with fire cautery, then heat the cautery clamps both very small and very large, according to what is suitable for the limb or the illness; after cauterizing all parts until you eradicate all corruption, leave nothing of it, so that everything that is corrupted is removed.

And this mixture is sometimes cured with hot medicine instead of fire cautery; but nevertheless, the fire cautery provides greater aid, and I have already described the treatment with hot medicine in detail: take it as needed.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	from the liquids that come as pieces
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Often it happens that pieces from a defect give rise to a disease called "close" according to our understanding, and it is a great wrong that hurts the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cautery for this disease is according to two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	This is to know, the cautery of fire, and the cautery of hot water.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	For the fire cautery, take a heated cheveit (iron) as thin as a feather of a kite, and make it of good iron to pierce the nail from all sides, and have subtle margins; then place it hot on the nail, and turn your hand around the nail until it reaches the bottom of the nail; leave it thus for three days until it begins to rot; then make an ointment with wild malves ground with silk, and leave the ointment on all night, and the nail will split and be pulled out from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then apply the clean dressing, covering it with cloth, as long as it is healthy.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	And if they are moved by heat, the body's strength is often broken and many times it happens in the hands and feet; so you must apply hot water cautery to them; and it is done like this: take a rod of iron or bronze, or a nail file, and attach the hot metal to a handle with cloth, that is to say, around the verrues; then place the rod on it so that it covers all around, then add a little hot water, and hold your hand tightly, pressing your hand while turning so that the edge of the rod reaches the base of the nail, and can find the hot water path deeply down to the root; and allow the patient to bear the sting of the hot water for an hour; then leave it like this, and it will come out at all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	First, make one after another, until you have freed all those that are in the body, then treat the injuries that cause pain.
li cure dou trembler	It cures the shaking of the body.
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	When anyone shivers from cold or quartan fever or any other ailment, it is necessary to perform four cauterizations or five on the spine of the back, one cauterization between each spine; and also one cauterization on the fish (a specific body part, possibly a nerve) and one on the stomach with an olive cautery. This will stop the trembling and hasten the healing from the cold illness.
des pustules puans	from pus-filled blisters

si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	if it is necessary to treat them at the first appearance that one makes a burn on each head of the pustule: a delicate burn with fir wood, from which the tip is seized by fire, or with long roots of herbs, or with a lenticular burn.
